linguas="af am ar as ast az be bg bn bn_IN br bs ca ca@valencia cs cy da de dz el en_CA en_GB en@shaw eo es et eu fa fi fr ga gl gu he hi hr hu id is it ja ka kn ko ku li lt lv mai mg mk ml mn mr ms nb ne nl nn nso oc or pa pl ps pt pt_BR ro ru rw si sk sl sq sr sr@latin sr@ije sv ta te th tr ug uk vi wa xh yi zh_CN zh_HK zh_TW zu "; \
for lang in $linguas; do \
  dir=/tmp/libbonoboui/pkg/libbonoboui/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/libbonoboui/src/libbonoboui-2.24.5/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/libbonoboui-2.0.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/libbonoboui-2.0.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/libbonoboui-2.0.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/libbonoboui-2.0.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/libbonoboui-2.0.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/libbonoboui-2.0.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/libbonoboui-2.0.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/libbonoboui-2.0.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
